    summary: 'Technology Pilots in Tanishq Store',
    description: 'Hi\nIn line with our charter of enhancing customer experience using Technology, CTS is evaluating a multitude of possibilities in this space. While some of them are still in preliminary exploration stage, ex : Virtual stores, a few of them have crossed into piloting stage. Many of you are aware of these projects, in a broad sense but perhaps not in great detail and some of you are not. Find below a list of projects, with a very brief introduction to the features, which are to be piloted this month. This invite is for a more elaborate presentation and discussion on these pilots.\nRequest your participation.\nIrys – Pilot from July 13th 2015\n RFID technology offers unique possibilities to the challenges facing the jewellery industry. Instantaneous, non – line –of –sight scanning capability means we no longer need to waste time and energy manually accounting for jewellery items, one piece at a time. With implementation of RFID, we can instantly scan/detect batches of jewellery items all at once.\n\nThe convenience of the solution from Irys offers monitoring jewellery items every day of the week, thereby keeping a check of items on a regular basis.\n The key Highlights of the solution:\n Portable Bluetooth RFID Handheld reader – The scanner can detect up to 100 items within 1-2 seconds, and the same info is transferred on to the Tablet where the complete product details are available. The same scanner can detect the missing items in the counter and display the details regarding the missing items.\nThe same scanner can be used in the other way to detect any missing item, all we need to do is to feed in the product code and run the scanner on all the counters. A simple beep is heard on the scanner once the item is found.\n Smart Tray – The scanner is placed on a tray where the customer can place all her shortlisted items; the application will display a comparative sheet which will aid the buying decision of the customer.\n Billing Time Reduction -   Interestingly we can use the Irys application to display product catalogs used as a Q buster in the store and the same reader can be used to do billing at the counter itself by connecting to our POS station.\n\nPurple Tab – Virtual Try on ( Pilot in July )\n\nDigital Catalog - Allows customers to browse through the entire product range including new launches.\n\nVirtual Trial Room - This is an interesting feature where customers can try numerous products virtually, where Ipad becomes a magical mirror. The key advantage will be with products like Nose pin where they are unable to try due to hygiene constraints can now have a feel of the product and similar is the case with Bangles a complete 360 degree view is available to the customer.\nStock Management – Any short listed item from the application can be directly billed and replenishment can happen automatically on integration with our back end ERP.\n\n\nFace First – Face Recognition (pilot on July 15 2015)\n\nRecognition of HNI Customers - Recognition of HNI customers across all touch points of Tanishq, where his past purchase history and preferences are available on a Tablet to the Store Manager or the Greeter.\n',
